## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# big-code-flink-arch-001: Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture

## Task

Map the Flink checkpoint coordination architecture: how the JobManager triggers a checkpoint, propagates barriers through the task graph, and coordinates acknowledgments. Trace the complete distributed two-phase commit from CheckpointCoordinator through barrier injection, barrier alignment/processing at downstream tasks, state snapshot, acknowledgment, to CompletedCheckpoint.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc (mirror of apache/flink) (Java, ~3.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Architectural Understanding
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: flink-runtime/checkpoint/ and flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/

## Requirements

1. Identify all relevant components in the checkpoint coordination flow (JobManager-side coordinator, RPC dispatch, barrier events, barrier handlers, state snapshot, acknowledgment)
2. Trace the dependency chain from CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint() through barrier propagation to CompletedCheckpoint
3. Document the aligned vs unaligned checkpoint barrier handling (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler vs CheckpointBarrierTracker)
4. Explain the PendingCheckpoint lifecycle and the ack-based completion protocol

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — role in architecture
- path/to/file2.ext — role in architecture
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Entry point: path/to/entry.ext
2. Calls: path/to/next.ext (via function/method name)
3. Delegates to: path/to/impl.ext
...

## Analysis
[Detailed architectural analysis including:
- Design patterns identified
- Component responsibilities
- Data flow description
- Interface contracts between components]

## Summary
[Concise 2-3 sentence summary answering the task question]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File recall: Did you find the correct set of architecturally relevant files?
- Dependency accuracy: Did you trace the correct dependency/call chain?
- Architectural coherence: Did you correctly identify the design patterns and component relationships?

The solution has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture — Summary

### Core Flow (Distributed 2PC)

**Phase 1 — Trigger & Barrier Propagation:**
1. `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()` creates a `PendingCheckpoint` (tracking all un-acked tasks) and sends trigger RPCs to source tasks via `Execution` → `TaskManagerGateway`.
2. Each `StreamTask` delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()`, which: (a) broadcasts a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream through output buffers, (b) takes a synchronous state snapshot via `operatorChain.snapshotState()`, (c) submits an `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` that sends `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC back to the JobManager upon completion.
3. The barrier flows through the network; downstream tasks receive it via `CheckpointedInputGate` → `CheckpointBarrierHandler`.

**Phase 2 — Ack Collection & Completion:**
4. `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` calls `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()` for each arriving ACK. When `isFullyAcknowledged()`, it calls `completePendingCheckpoint()` → `finalizeCheckpoint()` → persists `CompletedCheckpoint` → `sendAcknowledgeMessages()` (tasks commit external state).

### Aligned vs Unaligned Barrier Handling

| Handler | Semantics | Blocking | Implementation |
|---|---|---|---|
| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned) | Exactly-once | Blocks channels after barrier arrival; waits for all channels | `WaitingForFirstBarrier` → `CollectingBarriers` state machine |
| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (unaligned) | Exactly-once | No blocking; triggers on first barrier; captures in-flight buffers via `ChannelStateWriter` | `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned` state |
| `CheckpointBarrierTrac
... (truncated)

  "content": "# Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture\n\n## Files Examined\n\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java` \u2014 JobManager-side coordinator: triggers checkpoints, collects acknowledgements, drives PendingCheckpoint \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint lifecycle\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/PendingCheckpoint.java` \u2014 In-flight checkpoint tracking: holds notYetAcknowledgedTasks, accumulates subtask states, checks isFullyAcknowledged()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CompletedCheckpoint.java` \u2014 Finalized, persisted checkpoint containing all operator states after full acknowledgement\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/executiongraph/Execution.java` \u2014 Per-execution RPC dispatch: Execution.triggerCheckpoint() \u2192 TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/io/network/api/CheckpointBarrier.java` \u2014 Network event carrying checkpointId, timestamp, and CheckpointOptions propagated through operator graph\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/StreamTask.java` \u2014 Task runtime: receives RPC, calls performCheckpoint() \u2192 subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState(); also implements triggerCheckpointOnBarrier() and abortCheckpointOnBarrier()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java` \u2014 Task-local checkpoint orchestration: broadcasts barrier downstream, calls takeSnapshotSync (operatorChain.snapshotState()), then finishAndReportAsync (AsyncCheckpointRunnable)\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierHandler.java` \u2014 Abstract base for barrier handling: notifyCheckpoint() \u2192 toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(), notifyAbort()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java` \u2014 Aligned and unaligned checkpoint barrier handler: tracks a single in-flight checkpoint, blocks channels (aligned) or passes through (unaligned), uses BarrierHandlerState state machine\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierTracker.java` \u2014 At-least-once barrier handler: tracks barriers across multiple concurrent checkpoint IDs, does not block channels\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointedInputGate.java` \u2014 Wraps InputGate; intercepts incoming CheckpointBarrier events and delegates to CheckpointBarrierHandler\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/InputProcessorUtil.java` \u2014 Factory that creates CheckpointBarrierHandler (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler or CheckpointBarrierTracker) and wraps it in CheckpointedInputGate\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/BarrierHandlerState.java` \u2014 State machine interface for SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler; implementations: WaitingForFirstBarrier, AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier, AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinatorGateway.java` \u2014 RPC interface on JobManager accepting acknowledgeCheckpoint / declineCheckpoint from TaskManagers\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/RuntimeEnvironment.java` \u2014 Task-side environment: acknowledgeCheckpoint() sends AcknowledgeCheckpoint RPC message back to JobManager\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.java` \u2014 Coordinates operator-coordinator checkpointing in parallel with task checkpointing\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/DefaultCheckpointPlanCalculator.java` \u2014 Computes which tasks trigger, which wait-for-ack, and which commit\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Entry point**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:573` \u2014 `triggerCheckpoint(boolean isPeriodic)` is called periodically by a scheduled timer (or externally for savepoints).\n\n2. **Request routing**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:626` \u2014 `chooseRequestToExecute(request).ifPresent(this::startTriggeringCheckpoint)` queues or immediately executes the trigger request through `CheckpointRequestDecider`.\n\n3. **Plan calculation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:642` \u2014 `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` (`DefaultCheckpointPlanCalculator`) determines `tasksToTrigger` (sources), `tasksToWaitFor` (all tasks needing to ack), and `tasksToCommitTo`.\n\n4. **PendingCheckpoint creation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:901` \u2014 `createPendingCheckpoint(...)` instantiates a `PendingCheckpoint` with the set `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from the plan, schedules a timeout canceller, and inserts it into `pendingCheckpoints` map.\n\n5. **Coordinator & master hook snapshots**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:708,736` \u2014 `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion(...)` and `snapshotMasterState(checkpoint)` run asynchronously before task triggers.\n\n6. **RPC dispatch to source tasks**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:858,864` \u2014 `triggerTasks()` iterates `checkpoint.getCheckpointPlan().getTasksToTrigger()` and calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`.\n\n7. **RPC to TaskManager**: `Execution.java:1096` \u2014 `slot.getTaskManagerGateway().triggerCheckpoint(attemptId, jobId, checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)` \u2014 actual RPC message to the remote TaskManager.\n\n8. **Task receives trigger**: `StreamTask.java:1459` \u2014 `performCheckpoint()` \u2192 `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState(checkpointMetaData, checkpointOptions, checkpointMetrics, operatorChain, ...)`.\n\n9. **Barrier broadcast** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:333,344`):\n   - Step 1: `operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier(checkpointId)` \u2014 pre-barrier operator work\n   - Step 2: `operatorChain.broadcastEvent(new CheckpointBarrier(id, ts, options), isUnaligned)` \u2014 injects barrier into output buffers, flowing downstream through the network\n\n10. **Barrier reception at downstream task**: `CheckpointedInputGate` intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` from `InputGate` and calls `barrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, false)`.\n\n11. **Barrier alignment / tracking** (two implementations):\n    - **`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()`** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java:214`) \u2014 For exactly-once: tracks aligned channels; for aligned mode, blocks channels after first barrier (backpressure); for unaligned mode triggers immediately on first barrier announcement. Uses `BarrierHandlerState` state machine transitions. When all channels aligned: `allBarriersReceivedFuture.complete(null)` and `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n    - **`CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier()`** (`CheckpointBarrierTracker.java:94`) \u2014 For at-least-once: never blocks channels; tracks `CheckpointBarrierCount` per checkpoint ID; when count reaches target calls `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` \u2192 `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n\n12. **Downstream task checkpoint trigger**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` (`CheckpointBarrierHandler.java:147`) \u2192 `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(checkpointMetaData, options, metrics)` \u2192 `StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` \u2192 `performCheckpoint()` \u2192 same `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()` flow as step 8 (recursively propagating the barrier further downstream).\n\n13. **State snapshot** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:725`):\n    - `takeSnapshotSync()` calls `operatorChain.snapshotState(snapshotFutures, ...)` which calls each operator's `snapshotState()` synchronously (for RocksDB incremental) or initiates async writes.\n    - `finishAndReportAsync()` creates an `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` submitted to `asyncOperationsThreadPool` which waits for all `OperatorSnapshotFutures` to complete.\n\n14. **ACK sent to JobManager**: `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` upon completion calls `env.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, checkpointMetrics, taskStateSnapshot)` \u2192 `RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()` \u2192 sends `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC message to the JobManager.\n\n15. **Coordinator receives ACK**: `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1210`) \u2014 acquires coordinator lock, calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` (`PendingCheckpoint.java`).\n\n16. **Completion check**: If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` (tasks + operator coordinators + master states all acked), calls `completePendingCheckpoint(checkpoint)`.\n\n17. **Checkpoint finalization** (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1365`):\n    - `finalizeCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)` serializes metadata and creates `CompletedCheckpoint`\n    - `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest(...)` persists to `CompletedCheckpointStore` (ZooKeeper/filesystem HA)\n    - `onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)` \u2014 resolves the future returned from `triggerCheckpoint()`\n    - `sendAcknowledgeMessages(tasksToCommitTo, checkpointId, ...)` \u2014 notifies all tasks of checkpoint completion so they can commit (e.g., Kafka sink 2PC commit)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**:\nThe entire checkpoint protocol follows a distributed 2PC pattern. Phase 1 (prepare/vote): coordinator triggers, tasks snapshot state and send ACK. Phase 2 (commit): once all ACKs received, coordinator finalizes `CompletedCheckpoint` and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks (who then commit external sinks). Abort is possible if any task declines or times out.\n\n**State Machine for Barrier Handling**:\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses `BarrierHandlerState` as a strategy/state-machine pattern. States include `WaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingCollectingBarriers`, `CollectingBarriers` etc. \u2014 each implementing `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, and `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` transitions. This enables the \"alternating checkpoint\" mode which dynamically switches between aligned and unaligned based on alignment timeout.\n\n**Observer / Listener**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds a reference to `CheckpointableTask toNotifyOnCheckpoint`. When barriers are complete, it calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` \u2014 a push notification to the task. Similarly, `CheckpointCoordinator` acts as the observer for `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` messages.\n\n**Async Pipeline**:\n`startTriggeringCheckpoint()` is structured as a `CompletableFuture` pipeline: plan \u2192 ID allocation \u2192 PendingCheckpoint \u2192 storage location initialization \u2192 coordinator checkpoints \u2192 master hooks \u2192 `triggerCheckpointRequest()`. This avoids blocking the checkpoint timer thread.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Central orchestrator (JobManager side): triggers, tracks pending checkpoints, collects ACKs, finalizes/aborts, manages timeout |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight checkpoint state: tracks which tasks/coordinators have not yet acknowledged |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint with all state handles; persisted to HA store |\n| `Execution` | Proxy for a running task; dispatches checkpoint RPC via `TaskManagerGateway` |\n| `StreamTask` | Task runtime; receives trigger RPC, delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`; receives barrier callbacks from `CheckpointBarrierHandler` |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-local coordinator: broadcasts barrier, orchestrates operator snapshot, launches async finalization |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input gate wrapper that intercepts checkpoint barrier events from network |\n| `CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) | Reacts to barriers, manages alignment timing, notifies task when checkpoint can be taken |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier handler (aligned or unaligned); blocks channels during alignment; state machine driven |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier handler; tracks multiple concurrent checkpoints without blocking |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Off-thread async snapshot completion; sends ACK to JobManager upon success |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nJobManager timer\n    \u2192 CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n    \u2192 [creates PendingCheckpoint, calculates CheckpointPlan]\n    \u2192 [triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints + master hooks]\n    \u2192 Execution.triggerCheckpoint() [for each source task]\n        \u2192 TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint() [RPC]\n            \u2192 StreamTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()\n                \u2192 SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n                    \u2192 operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)\n                        \u2192 [barrier flows through output buffers to network]\n                    \u2192 takeSnapshotSync() [operator state snapshot]\n                    \u2192 finishAndReportAsync() \u2192 AsyncCheckpointRunnable\n                        \u2192 env.acknowledgeCheckpoint() [RPC back to JM]\n\n[Barrier flows through network channels to downstream tasks]\n    \u2192 CheckpointedInputGate intercepts CheckpointBarrier\n        \u2192 CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n            [Aligned / SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler]:\n                \u2192 waits for barriers from ALL input channels\n                \u2192 blocks channels that have sent barrier (backpressure)\n                \u2192 when all received: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n                    \u2192 StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n                        \u2192 same snapshot flow as above\n            [At-least-once / CheckpointBarrierTracker]:\n                \u2192 counts received barriers per checkpoint ID\n                \u2192 does NOT block channels\n                \u2192 when all received: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n\nJobManager receives AcknowledgeCheckpoint messages:\n    \u2192 CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        \u2192 PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n        \u2192 if isFullyAcknowledged():\n            \u2192 completePendingCheckpoint()\n                \u2192 finalizeCheckpoint() \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint\n                \u2192 CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpointAndSubsumeOldest()\n                \u2192 sendAcknowledgeMessages() [notify tasks: commit external state]\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **`CheckpointableTask`** (implemented by `StreamTask`): the interface `CheckpointBarrierHandler` uses to notify tasks \u2014 `triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` and `abortCheckpointOnBarrier()`.\n- **`TaskManagerGateway`**: RPC interface between Execution (coordinator side) and remote task; carries `triggerCheckpoint()`.\n- **`CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`**: RPC interface on JobManager for tasks to send `acknowledgeCheckpoint()` and `declineCheckpoint()`.\n- **`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator`**: interface between `StreamTask` and `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`, exposing `checkpointState()`, `notifyCheckpointComplete()`, `abortCheckpointOnBarrier()`.\n- **`BarrierHandlerState`**: strategy interface used by `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` for state transitions; implementations encapsulate alignment logic.\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Barrier Handling\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned(...)` with initial state `WaitingForFirstBarrier`.\n- On first barrier: starts alignment timer, blocks the channel (backpressure). Records it in `alignedChannels`.\n- Subsequent channels: blocks each as their barrier arrives.\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: calls `notifyCheckpoint()` \u2192 task snapshots state with no in-flight records crossing the barrier.\n- Guarantees exactly-once: no records between pre- and post-barrier data mix.\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (unaligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.unaligned(...)` with state `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`.\n- On first barrier announcement: immediately triggers checkpoint (calls `notifyCheckpoint`). Does NOT block channels.\n- In-flight channel buffers are snapshotted as part of channel state (via `ChannelStateWriter`) \u2014 records in-transit are included in the checkpoint.\n- Much lower latency under backpressure since channels never stall.\n\n**Alternating mode** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating(...)`):\n- Starts as aligned but if alignment exceeds `alignedCheckpointTimeout`, converts to unaligned via `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` state transition.\n\n**`CheckpointBarrierTracker`** (at-least-once):\n- Never blocks channels; maintains a queue of `CheckpointBarrierCount` objects tracking how many channels have sent each checkpoint's barrier.\n- Supports multiple concurrent in-flight checkpoints (up to `MAX_CHECKPOINTS_TO_TRACK = 50`).\n- When all channels for a checkpoint ID have been seen, fires `notifyCheckpoint()`.\n- Does not prevent records from mixing across checkpoint boundaries \u2192 at-least-once semantics only.\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n1. **Created**: `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint()` \u2014 sets `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from `checkpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`, schedules timeout via `CheckpointCanceller`.\n2. **Progressing**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` message calls `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` \u2014 moves task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` to `acknowledgedTasks`, stores `OperatorSubtaskState` in `operatorStates` map.\n3. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = `areTasksFullyAcknowledged() && areCoordinatorsFullyAcknowledged() && areMasterStatesFullyAcknowledged()`. Triggers `completePendingCheckpoint()`.\n4. **Completed**: Converted to `CompletedCheckpoint` via `finalizeCheckpoint()`, which writes checkpoint metadata to storage. Removed from `pendingCheckpoints` map.\n5. **Discarded/Aborted**: Via `abortPendingCheckpoint()` on timeout (`CheckpointCanceller`) or task decline (`DeclineCheckpoint` message) \u2014 canceller handle is used to cancel the timeout, state handles are discarded, `onCompletionPromise` is failed.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit: the `CheckpointCoordinator` (JobManager) triggers checkpoints by sending RPC calls to source tasks via `Execution.triggerCheckpoint()` \u2192 `TaskManagerGateway`, which causes each `StreamTask` to broadcast a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream through its output buffers via `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`. Downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate`, with `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` providing exactly-once semantics by blocking channels until all barriers are aligned (or triggering immediately for unaligned checkpoints), while `CheckpointBarrierTracker` provides at-least-once semantics without blocking. Each task snapshots operator state asynchronously and sends an `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC back to `CheckpointCoordinator`, which tracks progress in `PendingCheckpoint`; once all tasks and operator coordinators have acknowledged, `completePendingCheckpoint()` finalizes the `CompletedCheckpoint` in the HA store and broadcasts completion notifications so external sinks can commit their transactions.\n",

Phase 1 (prepare): coordinator sends trigger RPCs, tasks snapshot state and send ACK. Phase 2 (commit): once all ACKs received, coordinator persists `CompletedCheckpoint` and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks, which commit external state (e.g., Kafka offsets). Abort is triggered by task declines, failures, or timeout.\n\n**State Machine for Barrier Handling**:\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses `BarrierHandlerState` as a strategy/state-machine. States (`WaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`, `CollectingBarriers`) implement `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, and `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` transitions. Avoids blocking the checkpoint timer thread.\n\n**Template Method**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) defines the notification protocol (`notifyCheckpoint`, `notifyAbort`, alignment tracking) while leaving `processBarrier()`, `processBarrierAnnouncement()`, and `isCheckpointPending()` abstract for `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` and `CheckpointBarrierTracker`.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Central orchestrator (JobManager): triggers, tracks pending, collects ACKs, finalizes/aborts, manages timeout |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight state: tracks un-acked tasks/coordinators/master states, accumulates `OperatorSubtaskState` |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint with all state handles; persisted to HA store |\n| `Execution` | Proxy for a running task; dispatches checkpoint RPC via `TaskManagerGateway` |\n| `StreamTask` | Task runtime; receives trigger RPC, delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`; receives barrier callbacks |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-local coordinator: broadcasts barrier, orchestrates operator snapshot, launches async finalization |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input gate wrapper intercepting `CheckpointBarrier` events from the network |\n| `CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) | Reacts to barriers, manages alignment timing, notifies task when checkpoint can proceed |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier handler (aligned/unaligned/alternating); state machine driven |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier handler; tracks multiple concurrent checkpoints without blocking |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Off-thread async snapshot completion; sends ACK to JobManager upon success |\n\n### Data Flow\n\n```\nJobManager timer\n    \u2192 CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n    \u2192 [creates PendingCheckpoint, CheckpointPlan]\n    \u2192 JobManager]\n\n[Barrier arrives at downstream task via CheckpointedInputGate]\n    \u2192 CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / aligned]:\n            \u2192 blocks channel, records in alignedChannels\n            \u2192 when all channels aligned: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n                \u2192 StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n                    \u2192 same snapshot + broadcast + ACK flow\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / unaligned]:\n            \u2192 triggers immediately on first barrier (announcement)\n            \u2192 snapshots in-flight channel buffers via ChannelStateWriter\n        [CheckpointBarrierTracker / at-least-once]:\n            \u2192 counts barriers, no blocking\n            \u2192 when all seen: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n\nJobManager collects AcknowledgeCheckpoint messages:\n    \u2192 CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        \u2192 PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n        \u2192 if isFullyAcknowledged():\n            \u2192 completePendingCheckpoint()\n                \u2192 finalizeCheckpoint() \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint\n                \u2192 CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint()\n                \u2192 sendAcknowledgeMessages() [tasks commit external state]\n```\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Barrier Handling\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned(...)` with initial state `WaitingForFirstBarrier`.\n- On first barrier from any channel: starts alignment timer, records channel in `alignedChannels`, blocks that channel (backpressure via `CheckpointableInput`).\n- Subsequent barriers from other channels: each is blocked in turn.\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: calls `notifyCheckpoint()`. Task snapshots state with a clean cut \u2014 no records cross the barrier boundary.\n- Guarantees exactly-once: pre-barrier and post-barrier records are never mixed.\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (unaligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.unaligned(...)` with state `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`.\n- On first barrier announcement: immediately triggers checkpoint (`notifyCheckpoint()`). Does NOT block channels.\n- In-flight buffers in all channels are snapshotted as channel state via `ChannelStateWriter` \u2014 records in transit are included in the checkpoint.\n- Much lower checkpoint latency under backpressure since no channel stalling occurs.\n\n**Alternating mode** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating(...)`):\n- Starts as aligned but converts to unaligned if `alignedCheckpointTimeout` elapses, via `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` state transition.\n\n**`CheckpointBarrierTracker`** (at-least-once):\n- Never blocks channels; maintains `ArrayDeque<CheckpointBarrierCount>` tracking received barrier count per checkpoint ID.\n- Supports multiple concurrent in-flight checkpoints (up to `MAX_CHECKPOINTS_TO_TRACK = 50`).\n- When all channels for a checkpoint ID have sent their barrier, fires `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` \u2192 `notifyCheckpoint()`.\n- Does not prevent records from flowing across the checkpoint boundary \u2192 at-least-once semantics only.\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle and Ack-Based Completion Protocol\n\n1. **Created**: `createPendingCheckpoint()` \u2014 `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` populated from `checkpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`; timeout canceller scheduled.\n2. **Progressing**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` message \u2192 `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` moves task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` to `acknowledgedTasks`, stores `OperatorSubtaskState` in `operatorStates` map. Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult.SUCCESS` (or `DUPLICATE`/`UNKNOWN`/`DISCARDED`).\n3. **Coordinator acks**: `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints` calls `pendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeCoordinatorState()` for each coordinator completing its snapshot; tracked in `notYetAcknowledgedOperatorCoordinators`.\n4. **Master state acks**: `snapshotMasterState()` calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeMasterState(identifier, state)` for each master hook.\n5. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = `areTasksFullyAcknowledged() && areCoordinatorsFullyAcknowledged() && areMasterStatesFullyAcknowledged()` \u2192 triggers `completePendingCheckpoint()`.\n6. **Completed**: `finalizeCheckpoint()` serializes and persists checkpoint metadata; `PendingCheckpoint` is disposed; `CompletedCheckpoint` added to store and returned.\n7. **Aborted/Discarded**: `abortPendingCheckpoint()` on timeout or task decline \u2014 `CheckpointCanceller` fires, state handles discarded, `onCompletionPromise` completed exceptionally, `CancelCheckpointMarker` broadcast to downstream.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit driven by `CheckpointCoordinator` on the JobManager: it triggers checkpoints by sending RPCs to source tasks via `Execution` \u2192 `TaskManagerGateway`, which causes each `StreamTask` (via `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`) to broadcast a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream through its output buffers while simultaneously taking an async state snapshot. Downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate` and `CheckpointBarrierHandler` \u2014 `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` provides exactly-once by blocking channels until all barriers align (or triggers immediately for unaligned checkpoints with in-flight buffer capture), while `CheckpointBarrierTracker` provides at-least-once by counting barriers without blocking. Once all tasks send `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPCs, `CheckpointCoordinator` transitions the `PendingCheckpoint` to a `CompletedCheckpoint` persisted in the HA store and broadcasts completion notifications so external sinks can commit their transactions, completing the 2PC protocol.\n",

`tasksToWaitFor` (all tasks needing to ack), and `tasksToCommitTo`.\n\n4. **PendingCheckpoint creation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:901` \u2014 `createPendingCheckpoint(...)` instantiates combined into `masterTriggerCompletionPromise` before dispatching to tasks.\n\n6. **RPC dispatch to source tasks**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:836-867` \u2014 `triggerTasks()` iterates Step (2): `operatorChain.broadcastEvent(new CheckpointBarrier(id, ts, options), isUnaligned)` \u2014 injects barrier into all output buffers, flowing to downstream tasks through the network\n\n10. **Barrier reception at downstream task**: `CheckpointedInputGate` intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` arriving from `InputGate` channels and calls `barrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, false)`.\n\n11. **Barrier alignment / tracking** (two implementations):\n    - **`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()`** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java:214`) \u2014 Exactly-once: tracks `alignedChannels`; for aligned mode, blocks input channels after their barrier arrives (via `CheckpointableInput`); uses `BarrierHandlerState` for state machine transitions (`barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, `alignedCheckpointTimeout()`). When all channels aligned (`alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`): completes `allBarriersReceivedFuture`, calls `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n    - **`CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier()`** (`CheckpointBarrierTracker.java:94`) \u2014 At-least-once: never blocks channels; maintains `ArrayDeque<CheckpointBarrierCount>` per checkpoint; when `markChannelAligned()` count reaches target, calls `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` \u2192 `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n\n12. **Downstream task checkpoint trigger**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` (`CheckpointBarrierHandler.java:147`) \u2192 `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(checkpointMetaData, options, metrics)` \u2192 `StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` (`StreamTask.java:1396`) \u2192 `performCheckpoint()` \u2192 same `subtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()` flow, which in turn broadcasts the barrier further downstream (recursive propagation).\n\n13. **State snapshot** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:725`):\n    - `takeSnapshotSync()` calls `operatorChain.snapshotState(snapshotFutures, ...)` \u2014 each operator's `snapshotState()` runs synchronously for the metadata; actual state writing may be async.\n    - `finishAndReportAsync()` (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:690`) creates `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` submitted to `asyncOperationsThreadPool` which awaits all `OperatorSnapshotFutures`.\n\n14. **ACK sent to JobManager**: `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` upon completion calls `env.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, checkpointMetrics, taskStateSnapshot)` \u2192 `RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()` \u2192 sends `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC message to the JobManager's `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`.\n\n15. **Coordinator receives ACK**: `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1210`) \u2014 acquires coordinator lock, calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` on the `PendingCheckpoint`.\n\n16. **Completion check**: If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` (all tasks + operator coordinators + master states acked), calls `completePendingCheckpoint(checkpoint)`.\n\n17. **Checkpoint finalization** (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1365`):\n    - `finalizeCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)` serializes metadata, creates `CompletedCheckpoint`\n    - `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest(...)` persists to `CompletedCheckpointStore` (ZooKeeper or filesystem HA store); older checkpoints may be subsumed and discarded\n    - `onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)` \u2014 resolves the `CompletableFuture<CompletedCheckpoint>` returned from `triggerCheckpoint()`\n    - `sendAcknowledgeMessages(tasksToCommitTo, checkpointId, ...)` \u2014 notifies all committing tasks so they can call `notifyCheckpointComplete()` (e.g., Kafka sink 2PC commit)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Distributed Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**:\nThe checkpoint protocol mirrors 2PC exactly. Phase 1 (prepare): coordinator sends trigger RPCs, tasks snapshot state and send ACK. Phase 2 (commit): once all ACKs received, coordinator persists `CompletedCheckpoint` and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks, which commit external state (e.g., Kafka offsets). Abort is triggered by task declines, failures, or timeout.\n\n**State Machine for Barrier Handling**:\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses `BarrierHandlerState` as a strategy/state-machine. States (`WaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`, `CollectingBarriers`) implement `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, and `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` transitions. This enables the \"alternating checkpoint\" mode that dynamically switches between aligned and unaligned on alignment timeout.\n\n**Observer / Listener**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds `CheckpointableTask toNotifyOnCheckpoint`. When barriers complete, it calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`. `CheckpointCoordinator` observes `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC messages from all tasks.\n\n**Async Pipeline (CompletableFuture chaining)**:\n`startTriggeringCheckpoint()` is a `CompletableFuture` pipeline: plan calculation \u2192 ID allocation \u2192 `PendingCheckpoint` creation \u2192 storage location init \u2192 coordinator checkpoints \u2192 master hooks \u2192 `triggerCheckpointRequest()`. Avoids blocking the checkpoint timer thread.\n\n**Template Method**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) defines the notification protocol (`notifyCheckpoint`, `notifyAbort`, alignment tracking) while leaving `processBarrier()`, `processBarrierAnnouncement()`, and `isCheckpointPending()` abstract for `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` and `CheckpointBarrierTracker`.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Central orchestrator (JobManager): triggers, tracks pending, collects ACKs, finalizes/aborts, manages timeout |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight state: tracks un-acked tasks/coordinators/master states, accumulates `OperatorSubtaskState` |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint with all state handles; persisted to HA store |\n| `Execution` | Proxy for a running task; dispatches checkpoint RPC via `TaskManagerGateway` |\n| `StreamTask` | Task runtime; receives trigger RPC, delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`; receives barrier callbacks |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-local coordinator: broadcasts barrier, orchestrates operator snapshot, launches async finalization |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input gate wrapper intercepting `CheckpointBarrier` events from the network |\n| `CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) | Reacts to barriers, manages alignment timing, notifies task when checkpoint can proceed |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier handler (aligned/unaligned/alternating); state machine driven |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier handler; tracks multiple concurrent checkpoints without blocking |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Off-thread async snapshot completion; sends ACK to JobManager upon success |\n\n### Data Flow\n\n```\nJobManager timer\n    \u2192 CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n    \u2192 [creates PendingCheckpoint, CheckpointPlan]\n    \u2192 [triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints + master hooks]\n    \u2192 Execution.triggerCheckpoint() [for each source task]\n        \u2192 TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint() [RPC]\n            \u2192 StreamTask.performCheckpoint()\n                \u2192 SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n                    \u2192 operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()\n                    \u2192 operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)\n                        \u2192 [barrier flows downstream through network buffers]\n                    \u2192 takeSnapshotSync() \u2192 operatorChain.snapshotState()\n                    \u2192 finishAndReportAsync() \u2192 AsyncCheckpointRunnable\n                        \u2192 env.acknowledgeCheckpoint() [RPC \u2192 JobManager]\n\n[Barrier arrives at downstream task via CheckpointedInputGate]\n    \u2192 CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / aligned]:\n            \u2192 blocks channel, records in alignedChannels\n            \u2192 when all channels aligned: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n                \u2192 StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n                    \u2192 same snapshot + broadcast + ACK flow\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / unaligned]:\n            \u2192 triggers immediately on first barrier (announcement)\n            \u2192 snapshots in-flight channel buffers via ChannelStateWriter\n        [CheckpointBarrierTracker / at-least-once]:\n            \u2192 counts barriers, no blocking\n            \u2192 when all seen: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n\nJobManager collects AcknowledgeCheckpoint messages:\n    \u2192 CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        \u2192 PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n        \u2192 if isFullyAcknowledged():\n            \u2192 completePendingCheckpoint()\n                \u2192 finalizeCheckpoint() \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint\n                \u2192 CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint()\n                \u2192 sendAcknowledgeMessages() [tasks commit external state]\n```\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Barrier Handling\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned(...)` with initial state `WaitingForFirstBarrier`.\n- On first barrier from any
